### [36] [archived] 1. kAchit sUkshmatA apEXitaM.

**Created:** 7/24/2017 9:16:25 PM

**Created by:** Shruthi Viswanath



**Description:**

yadA ahaM uktavati aham shrAntA asmi iti, tadA anAvashyaka tOlanaM kritavAn (prAchina mahilAh, grAma mahilAh gItaM gAtvA kAryaM kuruvanti). ahaM "te samshOdhanaM na kuruvanti" iti uktavati. tadarthaM "tad kimapi mahat kAryaM kuruvanti asti iti na chintaya" iti uktavAn. tadanantaraM parishIlya, "tad bhavatu, tadapi gItaM gAtvA karaNIyaM, santOShena karaNIYam" iti uktavAn. mama kShInatAyA tOlanaM anAvshyakaM AsIt. tEbhyah api shishu Evam 24/7 bhavati chet tE api gItaM na gAtum shaknuvanti. taM gRRItvA 1.5 hrs athitavati, mahyaM na tyaktavAn sah. tad sarvaM na jnAtvA tatheiva BS vadasi.

#### Comments
**7/24/2017 9:29:58 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

sahanA, anukampa nAsti. prAyaH na apEXa api karaNIya. 

**7/24/2017 9:26:34 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

mama samIpe nyUnAti nyUnam sUkshmatA nAsti chet bahu asahyaM bhavati

**7/24/2017 9:25:55 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

tathA adya 30 mins pArk madhye madhyAhnaM sthanaM dattavati.

### [81] [archived] AchAraH log.

**Created:** 8/30/2017 10:29:55 AM

**Created by:** Shruthi Viswanath



**Description:**

shrutyAh vishvAsEna saha AchAra gamanaM. 
dhyEyaH: samskArAbhivRddHiH

#### Comments
**8/31/2017 4:28:45 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

asyedam nAsti sthAnam.

**8/30/2017 10:34:20 AM Shruthi Viswanath**

Aug 30, 8.15 am: 
SV: ahaM 6pm aagamishyAmi, sAyaM tvamEva pAlaya.
VV: yadi samayam asti.
SV: sarvadA samayaH na bhavishyati tava, tvayA karaNIyamEva, ahaMEva na kartum shaknomi.
VV: tvaM tyaktvA viLambEna aagaccha. aavaam katham pAlanIyam iti na vada, tava chintA mAstu. 
SV: tvaM kimchit api apatya pAlanaM na karOshi
VV: bahu karomi Eva, tava agre samarthanaM kartum mama utsAho nAsti. 
(ardhaM ardhaM shrutvA)

**Created:** 7/2/2018 3:47:05 PM

**Created by:** Shruthi Viswanath

**Due:** 11/30/2018 12:00:00 PM

#### Comments
**7/8/2018 1:47:39 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

Panorama kit ID (my.natera.com) 5135198-2-N

**7/4/2018 9:22:44 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

OMI Draw Station Mountain View
 (650) 691-8633
 
2500 Hospital Drive - Building 2
​Mountain View, CA 94040

Panorama 9am-3pm




**7/3/2018 12:49:54 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

For general knowledge, Healthnet PPO has no deductible, and 20% copay for X-ray, lab tests including genetic screening. 
Genetic screening CPT code 81420/81422. 
Interaction ID: (phone call reference): I-23485866

**7/3/2018 12:45:05 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

Progenity NIPT 

Sarah Mudgett , 408-309-3176, sarah.mudgett@progenity.com  
She said usually patients don't have to pay more than $185-$200. (If you get charged more than that, call our financial services and they will honor 185). You can get even lower potentially, since we have a sliding scale for low-income patients. You would have to call and ask that at the time of billing. And insurance may also cover you so that you pay less than that.

**7/3/2018 12:42:23 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

Natera (Panorama test)

Natera Area sales rep Mia kocer  5108286917
mkocer@natera.com

She said 150$ best price for low-income compassionate. 


**7/3/2018 11:27:13 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

@shruthiviswanath - talk to Natera - say insurance won't cover (age only 30 < 35). Ask for non-insurance deal, say that you earn low (55k per year). - "Please call us at 855.271.1502. "

(source - https://my.natera.com/pdfs/20170720-billing-faq.pdf https://www.natera.com/panorama-test/common-questions  )

Note: 
1. Landels has a YMCA preschool, no Landels preschool.
2. MVSchool  District preschools are in Thereukauf Elem and Castro Elem, not in Landels.
3. YMCA preschool is closed forsummer due to summercamp.
4. It needs the kid to be potty trained.
5. It usually doesnt fill up since it is 7.30-12 5x a week, and most people are lookingfor aftercare. 
6. Enrollment for Fall starts in May but you can enrol anytime since it doesnt fill up.
7. Sharon Winder swinder@ymcasv.org handles enrollment.

(1) get a form to be on the waitlist. (2) get an appointment to collect enrolment packet (3) fill the forms and get another appointment to complete admission.

You're transferring the vehicle to a:
Spouse or domestic partner.

**7/1/2018 1:59:37 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

Canara bank NEFT: 
https://canarabank.com/english/bank-services/personal-banking/technology-products/faq-on-neft/

Q3. What is NEFT- National Electronic Fund Transfer?

Ans: This system of fund transfer operates on a Deferred Net Settlement basis. Fund transfer transactions are settled in batches. Presently, NEFT operates in hourly batches from 8 am to 7 pm on week days and 8 am to 1 pm on Saturdays.
For example, currently, NEFT operates in hourly batches - there are twelve settlements from 8 am to 7 pm . Any transaction initiated after a designated settlement time would have to wait till the next designated settlement time 

For NEFT transaction there is no lower and upper value limit.

Ans: The remitting customer has to furnish the following information to a bank for effecting a NEFT and RTGS remittance:

1. Amount to be remitted

2. Remitting customer's account number which is to be debited

3. Name and IFS Code of the beneficiary bank

4. Name of the beneficiary customer

5. Account number of the beneficiary customer

6. Sender to receiver information, if any

7. Mobile number / email id (for NEFT to receive credit confirmation)

Service charges:
Rs. 10001/- to Rs. 1 lakh : Rs. 5.00

"If you pay your visa application fee with an electronic fund transfer from your bank account it can take up to 2 business days from the time of payment for your receipt to be activated, after which you may schedule the appointment." 

किञ्च काचित् "Meanwhile, the NEFT payment got activated automatically in 2.5 hours after transferring from my account. It was so easy and had no problems. 

You will receive an SMS and an email once the payment is activated together with the receipt number though you don't need to type the receipt number in the profile as it will be automatically populated.
" इत्यवदत् [अत्र](https://www.immihelp.com/forum/showthread.php/110286-Receipt-Number-for-NEFT-payment-transfer)।

अन्यत्र "CASH PAYMENT OF US VISA FEES - axis bank" इत्यस्मिन् - "Applicant can schedule your interview the next business day after paying your visa application fee. Receipt activation can take up to 2 business days from the time of payment."

**5/18/2018 2:46:17 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

"n response to your question, please note that, each visa applicant must independently meet the renewal category criteria to qualify for Interview Waiver (No Appointment)/ Interview Waiver (Biometric Appointment Only) if applicable. Family/group member not eligible for renewal category should apply individually. Please follow the link: http://www.ustraveldocs.com/in/in-niv-visarenew.asp for information regarding the eligibility criteria for the Interview Waiver (No Appointment)/ Interview Waiver (Biometric Appointment Only) for each applicant, as we will not be able to comment if applicants would qualify for the same.

Since, your spouse is applying for the first time he will not be eligible for Interview Waiver (No Appointment)/ Interview Waiver (Biometric Appointment Only) and apply separately. As per our records we see that your spouse is added as dependent on your profile. Hence, we request you to detach his details from your profile." इत्युत्तरम्।

 Each visa applicant, whether an individual, a dependant family member, or as part of a group, must independently meet the following criteria to qualify for interview waiver. http://www.ustraveldocs.com/in/in-niv-typework.asp#dependents : 
Your dependents should bring all required documents for any nonimmigrant visa, plus:

An original marriage (for your spouse) and/or birth certificate (for unmarried children under 21), as applicable
A letter from your spouse's employer confirming his or her continued employment
If your spouse is currently working in the United States on an H1-B visa, his/her pay slips for the current calendar year and federal tax returns (IRS Form 1040 and W-2s) for all the years in which he/she has been employed in the United States on the H-1B visa

**7/1/2018 5:07:03 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

"We don't offer joint personal accounts or small business accounts right now."

**7/1/2018 5:06:58 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

"Opening a digibank e-wallet takes less than 90 seconds. You can convert to a digiSavings account by completing your biometric authentication at any of our partner stores. "

Account opening requires initial OTP, but later not for regular operation, it seems.




**7/1/2018 5:03:35 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Rates and fees - https://www.dbs.com/digibank/in/rates-and-fees.html

e-wallet - no fees.

digiSavings - annual debit card fees. (150Rs  = 7% interest over 2000 or .03 post inflation growth over 4200)

e-wallet - no interest, no debit card.
digiSavings - 7% (compare with 4% CPI inflation rate.)

e-wallet does not have NEFT, IMPS ಇತಿ ಶ್ರುತಿಃ.

अग्रिम-मासय् इति निश्चितं ह्यः।

**2/26/2018 7:04:06 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

गर्भकारणाद् वान्तिर् भवति, तेन कार्यप्राप्तौ सन्दर्शने काठिन्यं स्याद् इति श्रुत्या तिरस्कृतम् अधुना।

**2/9/2018 9:46:05 AM Shruthi Viswanath**

adya manuscript progress andrej-yA saha drishtvA vadAmi.

**2/6/2018 12:09:13 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Jun, Jul, Aug इत्येतेषु गमनागमनम् द्वितीय-मासत्रयम् चेति चिन्तयामश्चेद् इदानीमेवोचितः समयः।

**2/6/2018 12:07:05 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

http://americanpregnancy.org/pregnancy-health/traveling-during-pregnancy/  इत्येवं वदति -

"Should You Travel at all During Your Pregnancy?
As long as there are no identified complications or concerns with your pregnancy, it is generally safe to travel at all times during your pregnancy. The ideal time to travel during pregnancy is the second trimester.  In most cases, you are past the morning sickness of the first trimester and several weeks from the third stage of pregnancy when you are more easily fatigued."

https://community.babycenter.com/post/a40144873/long_flight_while_pregnant इत्यप्युपयोगायास्ति। विशिष्य - 
"Also, carry a letter saying how far along you are and that the doctor clears you to fly, even if you're under the limit that requires the letter (usually 36 weeks). The airline may not even ask for one. I do know people who "showed" more and the airlines were worried they were past the deadline. Once they see the letter, legally, they're in the clear. " … "I completely, completely agree with the suggestion of support hose (I wore thigh highs, not just knee highs) and that you need to be measured for them at the medical gadget store.  You want as much support as possible, the kind that you have to turn inside out and slide up your legs instead of putting on like tights.  See if your OBGYN will give you a prescription for them if you think your insurance will help cover part of the cost."

**8/3/2017 5:31:30 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

इदानीम् नेत्युक्तम् अधुनैव स्पष्टतया, न पूर्वम्। साधु। चिन्ता नास्ति। पश्चाच् चिन्तयाव।

**8/3/2017 4:36:46 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

kati vAraM vaktavyaM?
- mama 3rd paper asya krute mahyaM data prAptvA samApanIyaM! no chet bahu viLambhaH bhavati.
- ahaM bhavishye kim samshodanaM karishyAmi iti na jAnAmi, dIrghaM chintanaM aavashyakaM. startup (mama lab) bootstrap kuruvanti asmi, mama shirasi bahu asti! tadanantaraM kartum shakyate, kAchit sahana AvashyakaM. Evam pressure na sthApaya. 

tvaM vinA kAraNam "pressure" na sthApaya. surrogate na bhavati, mayA Eva  karaNIyaM. yathEshtaM na kartuM arhasi.

**3/2/2018 11:15:01 AM Shruthi Viswanath**

TB test needed according to risk assessment questionaire. https://www.ctca.org/fileLibrary/file_574.pdf

Can be performed by physician, physician asst, nurse or nurse asst.

Costs $79 in sutter health 
https://www.sutterhealth.org/services/primary/walk-in-care-tb-test

Costs $25+28 in Walgreens https://www.walgreens.com/topic/healthcare-clinic/price-menu.jsp

Costs $35+30 in CVS
https://www.cvs.com/minuteclinic/services/price-lists

SFCC offers free vaccination and testing for people without insurance
https://sffc.org/primary-care/

#### Comments
**3/19/2018 10:57:17 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

arch is highly configurable. its wiki is rich - oft turns up first in searches.

offers easy installation of much software ( via the huge user repo). heavily slanted towards bleeding edge versions.

os installation is tough - but install scripts help.

**3/19/2018 10:52:58 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

manjaro had install problems.

**3/19/2018 10:51:37 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

mint had ibus problems. fctix worked better after coaxing - but goldendict needed updating for it.

**3/16/2018 8:27:06 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**


```
Section "InputClass"
        Identifier  "Marble Mouse"
        MatchProduct "Logitech USB Trackball"
        MatchIsPointer "on"
        MatchDevicePath "/dev/input/event*"
        Driver "evdev"
        Option "EmulateWheel" "true"
        Option "EmulateWheelButton" "9"
        Option "Emulate3Buttons" "true"
EndSection
​
```
which was working in Ubuntu, causes x11 to not start.

**2/26/2018 2:01:42 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

ahaM ~7-8 varShIyA Asam, parantu apI mahyam na rOchate sma, "separation". 

**2/26/2018 2:01:06 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

you are trying to provide a fringe benefit at the cost of having a major disadvantage. 

**2/26/2018 1:45:04 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

सर्वं पठितम्। 

सारोऽत्र -
- "**If such separation in early childhood is not well handled**, sensitive children may be emotionally disturbed for a considerable time afterwards. It is believed that children aged 6 months to 4 years are more particularly vulnerable. " इत्यस्मिन् "**separation can be well handled**" इत्यवगन्तव्यम् [अस्मात्](http://www.naturalchild.org/peter_cook/attachment.html)। 
- अपि [चात्र](https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC3115616/) - "We focus on separation between birth and age two because during that period children rely on physical proximity as the primary indicator of their mother’s availability. Mothers who have left the home environment, even if available by phone, are perceived as unavailable. Maternal availability is particularly important within the first two years of life because of the infant’s limited understanding of the reasons for maternal absence and the timing of her return. As a result, experiences of separation may be particularly salient. Even those as brief as a few hours in duration can result in distress. **By the third or fourth year of life, the child increasingly understands that his or her mother has motives and plans of her own, and their relationship develops into a “goal-corrected partnership” (Bowlby, 1969/1982). Open lines of communication between mother and child thus allow the child to perceive continuity in their relationship despite brief absences. As a result, separation anxiety typically declines markedly** (Kobak, Cassidy, Lyons-Ruth, & Ziv, 2006; Kobak & Madsen, 2008)." इत्यस्मिन्न् अन्तिमभागोऽधिगन्तव्यः। सुप्रत्ययस्यैतादृशी सुस्थितिर् जात एवेति ममानुभूतिः। नित्यं बहुवारं त्वया सह भाषिष्यत एव।
- तत्रैव - "As previously mentioned, the reason for the separation, where the child stayed, and who provided care are all potentially informative for helping to understand the effects of separation on parents and children. A maternal separation is quite likely not as distressing to an infant if he/she is left in the care of another attachment figure to whom he/she is securely attached. … Another important contextual factor for which we did not account is the quality of care that the child receives during the separation, which can greatly alter how stressful the separation is for the infant. Gunnar et al. (1992) found that infants who received continuous, responsive, and individualized care during a 30 minute separation were much less stressed by the situation than children who were merely comforted and then left to play independently. It is quite likely that the quality of the care and the responsiveness of the alternate caregiver predicts much of the variability in how children respond to separations."

**2/26/2018 10:45:59 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

सुप्रत्यय-भारतगमनकाले स्थूल-निश्चये चिन्तिताः विषयाः - 
- श्रुत्या भारतागमने विलम्बस्य निरीक्षा।
- भारतेषु बाल-परिसरो जनैः पूर्णः (अनेकजनसहत्वम् इच्छति बाल इत्य् अतिथ्यागमने तत्सम्भ्रमेण ज्ञायते) भवतितराम् (प्रथमस्, तत्परिवारः, मातुलपरिवारः, विश्वासपरिवारः, श्रुतिपरिवारः, परिवेशिबाला उद्यानागन्तारः, क्रीडाशाला) - न तावत् पर्वतदर्शनप्रदेशे (यद्यपि parenting coop इत्यादिकं सप्ताहे द्वित्रिवारं सम्भवति, यथा विद्यया सूचितम्)। 
- नानापरिसरेभ्यः सुप्रत्ययस्य प्रेषणम्।
- श्रुतिवियोगे सुप्रत्ययस्य सुखम् (तद्विरहे नित्यं बहु कालं यावद् वर्तत एव। पुराऽपि श्रुतिप्रयाणे सुखेनैवावर्तत)।
- सुप्रत्ययवियोगे श्रुति-दुःखम्। (दुःखम् भविष्यत्येव। तस्या असन्तोषप्रवृत्तिः प्रकृत्याऽत्यधिका। तथापि सुप्रत्यय-सन्तोषाभिवृद्धी ध्यात्वा तुष्येर् इति विश्वासः।)
- श्रुत्याः यथापेक्षं विरामदिनेषु दूरस्थकार्यदिनेषु भारतवासः।
- विश्वासस्य पर्यटकानुमत्या ऽमेरिकागमने शक्तिः सुप्रत्ययसहितस्य।
- जानक्य् असत्यवादिनी विश्वासविद्वेषिणी किञ्चिन्तयेद् इत्यपि विद्या।

विद्यानागरत्नाभ्यां व्यक्तिगतसूचना दत्ता श्रुति-विश्वासाभ्याम्। विश्वासेन ध्रुवं मध्यस्थथानं तिरस्कृत्यापि सूचनाः परिगणिताः। श्रुत्यनुज्ञा च लब्धा।

प्रतिगमनदिने सूक्ष्मनिश्चये चिन्तितानि - नागरत्ना-चीटिका-परिवर्तन-धनम्। विश्वासस्य प्रयाणे सुप्रत्ययस्य पालने शक्तिः। नानाप्रयाणदिनेषु व्ययः। h4 नवीकरणव्ययः। 
विश्वासगमनात्परम् नागरत्नाया विद्यागृहगमने सर्वेषाम् इच्छा शक्तिश्च।

**2/25/2018 2:29:49 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

अतः, @shruthiviswanath एन निश्चितम् - "निश्चितदिने विश्वासेन सह भारतं गच्छतु सुप्रत्ययः।" इति।

### [202] [archived] चौलदिने ब्राह्मणविधौ संशोधनम्

**Created:** 2/7/2018 10:24:56 AM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः

**Due:** 2/10/2018 12:00:00 PM

**Description:**

यत्पुण्य॒न्नक्ष॑त्रम् । तद्बट्कु॑र्वीतोपव्यु॒षम् । य॒दा वै सूर्य॑ उ॒देति॑ । अथ॒ नक्ष॑त्र॒न्नैति॑ । याव॑ति॒ तत्र॒ सूर्यो॒ गच्छे॑त् । यत्र॑ जघ॒न्यं॑ पश्ये॑त् । ताव॑ति कुर्वीत यत्का॒री स्यात् । पु॒ण्या॒ह ए॒व कु॑रुते । ए॒वं ह॒ वै य॒ज्ञेषु॑ञ्च श॒तद्यु॑म्नञ्च मा॒थ्स्यो नि॑रवसाय॒याञ्च॑कार ।। 6 ।।	2.1.5.2.1

#### Comments
**2/7/2018 10:58:41 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

कृत्तिकानक्षत्रं सदा विषुवसूर्योदयस्थाने स्याद् इति निश्चिनुमश्चेत् (यथा तैत्तिरीयब्राह्मणाविर्भाववेलायाम् आसीत्), तर्हि पुनर्वसुनक्षत्रं 53-60 = -7 deg equinoctial longitude इति  रेखायाम् आपतति।
निश्चिते दिने (Mar 25) सूर्योदयाद् ईषत् प्रागेव परिष्कृतनक्षत्रस्थानमेतद् (0deg latitude, -7 deg equinoctial longitude) उदेति।



**2/7/2018 10:26:49 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

सम्प्रति चान्द्रनक्षत्रम् एव स्वीक्रियत इति श्रीरमणः - https://twitter.com/agnimaan/status/961087719483981824 । 
मत्तूरुरामनारायणः पृष्टः।

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



#### Comments

**1/13/2018 4:21:39 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

http://exoticclassifieds.com/search-by-species/  इत्यन्ये सङ्केताः।

**1/13/2018 4:21:00 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Hello. All blackbuck skins start at $550 and go up from there. I don’t know of any customers who have recently taken them back to India that could help. I’m sorry. As far as I know, they all kept them here in the U.S
iti http://axisdeerhides.com/Axis_prayer_rugs.html

**1/13/2018 3:11:17 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Wildlife protection act http://www.moef.nic.in/legis/wildlife/wildlife1.html

"Certificate of ownership. - The Chief Wildlife Warden may, for the purposes of Sec. 40, issue a certificate of ownership in such form, as may be prescribed, to any person who, in his opinion, is in lawful possession of any wild animal or any animal article, trophy, or uncured trophy, and may, where possible, mark, in the prescribed manner, such animal article, trophy or uncured trophy for the purposes of Identification."

"According to Wildlife Protection Act, 1972 (WPA), only those skins and trophies that were acquired before 1972 and bequeathed or gifted are eligible for registration certificates. Also, if any dead animal is found in the wild, it can't be skinned. Neither can any body part be taken. It has to be burnt on the spot in the presence of an appointed representative of metropolitan court and witnesses."

Exotic animal skin import ban (doesn't seem to apply to black-bucks or non-traders) - https://hsi.org.au/blog/2017/02/19/india-bans-trade-in-exotic-animal-skins-and-fur/

ahaM chapati api bahishtAt aanayAmi parantu eshaH "samyak nAsti" iti na khAdati

**11/14/2017 4:31:22 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

aam, ahaM pointedly adya uktavati, cut vegetables aanayAmaha iti. saha " na ahaM kartum shaknomi, shrAntah na bhavAmi" iti uktavAn. ahaM hyaha pAkam kritavati athaH jAnAmi, svAnubhavEna, tad bahu tiring asti. itah paraM ahaM tasya chapAti na khAdAmi. supru api chapati na khAdati. yAvat shakyam sAyaM ahaMeva kimchit roti vA palya karishyAmi yadA nyUnam bhavati tasya shramaH

**11/14/2017 4:18:11 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

श्रुते, त्वं पितृनिर्मिता रोटिका न खादसि चेद् वरम्। सुप्रत्ययं त्यक्त्वा सायम् २० निमेषाणि रोटिका असृजत् (सङ्गणकस्याग्रे त्यक्तुं प्रायतत, अहं निरसेधम्)। तथा निराकरोषि चेत् केवलं स्वस्य सुप्रत्ययस्य च कृते तव पिता +अर्धम् एव समयं निर्माणे स्वीकरिष्यति।

@shruthiviswanath Exactly - penalty charge unless you inform them each time you use the car.

**11/5/2017 7:56:14 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

@vishvasah
Also asked on the website contact  form.
 The Metromile Pulse must be plugged into your car at all times so mileage can be accurately measured and billed. It also enables valuable features like the car locator and trip tracking. If it ever loses signal, try taking it out and plugging it back in. If this still doesn’t work, please let us know to avoid any penalty charges.

If you ever need a new device, you will be covered during the grace period while it is being mailed to you. It’s also OK to remove the Pulse when your car is being serviced, just be sure to plug it back in afterwards.

**11/5/2017 6:41:23 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

उर्जाकोशं निष्कासयाम इति कारणेन प्रायेण तेषां यन्त्रं स्तम्भितवाहने कार्यं न कुर्यात्। तथापि चिन्ता नास्ति वेति सम्यज् ज्ञातव्यम्। @shruthiviswanath 

**11/5/2017 6:37:14 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

https://www.metromile.com/rates

**11/5/2017 6:35:39 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

Will getting a quote with Metromile affect my credit score?
No, Metromile does a "soft pull" credit inquiry (in states where credit is used in your rate), which only reviews your insurance score, without lowering it. Soft pulls are not noted on your credit report except for listing the requester's name.

What is an insurance score?
This score uses much of the same credit information as a credit score, but is calculated a little differently to predict future car insurance claims. Please refer to the footer for more information regarding your insurance score.

**11/5/2017 6:33:57 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

320.50 savings per annum (note that vvasuki's claim was not entered in metromile and this may increase the premium)

**2/26/2018 10:36:42 AM Shruthi Viswanath**

IISER Pune: (1) your package will go through an initial internal screening which takes 6-8 months. The application committee meets every quarter. IISER Pune faculty meets every quarter to shortlist candidates : (e.g. Nov, Feb, May, Aug) .  
 (2) Then shortlist for interview, then seminar and visit the place. (3) Then selection committee with external reviewers. Offer within a month of selection committee meeting. 
Latest procedure http://www.iiserpune.ac.in/userfiles/files/POLICY%20&%20GUIDELINES%20-IISERP%20-07_12_2017.pdf

**2/26/2018 10:30:34 AM Shruthi Viswanath**

Institutes are happy to recommend candidates (who have indicated acceptance) for fellowships.

- IISER Pune

**2/26/2018 10:25:10 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

tarhi prAyeNa tava Oct-Dec ityantare nirNayaH.

**2/26/2018 9:26:52 AM Shruthi Viswanath**

IISc selection process and timeline (similar in IITs): 
(1) dept interviews candidate
(2) if dept likes candidate, sets up selection committee with dean, (usually a formality interview), 2people from dept etc. 
(3) this committee meets one week before the council which formally approves an offer. 
Council meetings are in March,June, Sept, Dec.

Total time from application to offer: 4-6 months. 

**2/21/2018 11:21:12 AM Shruthi Viswanath**

answers: https://docs.google.com/document/d/1Fyy0DctZFvENyJ0by5TO9di5qUIjvOgJiYNd1zHI_Gc/edit

**2/17/2018 3:13:40 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

"प्राध्यापकत्वप्रस्तावानन्तरम् अप्य् अमेरिकेषु भवितव्यम् वा?" इत्यस्मिन् चिन्ता मास्तु - भारतवासो ऽननुकूलश् चेदपि तत्सोढ्वा कार्यं लब्धुं यतिष्य इति श्रुतिः।

एवञ्च+अधिकं नाम+ आगस्ट्-१-इति दिनस्य परिसरे भारतप्राप्तिर् इति निश्चिता। ततः पूर्वमेव स्यादिति श्रुतिः॥

### [1] [archived] अपत्य-जनन-समये निश्चयः

**Created:** 7/9/2017 4:03:35 PM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



#### Comments
**7/12/2017 1:07:48 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

tarjanE kAchit sUkshmatA.

**7/12/2017 1:02:04 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

दुष्टे, शठे - https://docs.google.com/document/d/1jMgu6bY_rYr-m6x80_vSOOPb4TtzCP7Cgq13rryU-XA/edit <--- गतवर्षे त्वयैवाङ्गीकृते सन्धौ प्रथमबिन्दुम् पश्य - "dharmE nAshitE tarjanasya svikrti, chintana pUrvakaM doShasya angIkAra, bhaviShye sudhAraNasya pratijnA, उचित-प्रायश्चित्त+आचरणम्।"

धर्मस्योल्लङ्घनं कृत्वा किमन्यद् अपेक्षसे? दोषय् आचरिते शोधनाय तर्जनम् अङ्गीकरणीयम् इति धर्मः। पार्तेनियम्-विष-पादपस्य बीजम् उप्त्वा आम्रफलमिच्छसि? इतोऽपि चर्चितुम् इच्छसि चेद् अस्ति वादपत्त्रम्।

### [126] [archived] Register Hindu Undivided Family HUF

**Created:** 11/12/2017 9:51:49 PM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



**Description:**

prAyeNa pitrArjita-sampada eveti bhAti. 
Money or movable property received from relatives is not taxable.
Money or movable property received by a HUF from its members is not taxable.

#### Checklist

[ ] Register deed with gift - https://img.jagoinvestor.com/files/HUF-creation-deed.pdf

[ ] PAN app https://www.onlineservices.nsdl.com/paam/endUserRegisterContact.html

[ ] Open HUF bank account

[ ] Add HUF basics in notes

[ ] Open HUF brokerage account - https://upstox.com/files/Sample_NDFormA.pdf

#### Checklist - notes

[ ] Advantages

[ ] Formation - by status, not contract

[ ] coparcener - formerly males. a common male  ancestor and his lineal descendants within 4 degrees, running from and including such ancestor. Share in partition

[ ] members - married-in women. adapted kids. Right to maintenance.

[ ] Dissolution/ partition - Equal rights of members. Only coparceners can trigger.

[ ] Karta gifting property to daughter upon marriage

[ ] Gifts from the HUF to members and parents, grandparents, children, grandchildren, brothers and sisters, even uncles, aunties and in-laws

[ ] gift declarations

#### Comments
**11/20/2017 2:26:07 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Partition: "To constitute a partition all that is necessary is a definite and unequivocal indication of intention by a member of a joint family to separate himself from the family. "

**11/20/2017 1:47:35 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Risks:
 “Partition of real estate belonging to an HUF can be a nightmare, and more often than not, it leads to disputes and court cases,” said Bhatia.
"an HUF cannot be broken into parts; all members have to agree to dissolve an HUF. If an HUF has only a few members, things may run smoothly. Problems mostly appear when the number of coparceners increases. Since all lineal descendants are part of an HUF, every child, whether boy or girl, who gets added to the family, becomes a part of the HUF."

**11/20/2017 1:12:41 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

"Apart from getting tax deduction up to Rs. 1,00,000 for an individual, it is possible that if an HUF is created by that individual, he will be able to claim higher tax deduction and exemptions under the Income-tax Law because the new tax entity in the form of a Hindu Undivided Family will be eligible to claim separate tax deduction under section 80C of the Income-tax Act, 1961.  Likewise, the dividend income and the Long-term Capital Gains on listed securities would also be exempted for such Hindu Undivided Family.  The income from Short-term Capital Gain by this Hindu Undivided Family will also be eligible to a lower tax rate of 15 per cent tax only. " but - "Long-term capital gains arising on transfer of Equity shares or units of Equity Oriented Mutual Funds, liable to STT on sale, are exempt from tax." But, "Long term Capital Gain on Unlisted Shares in India/Foreign Company Shares ( - which can't be owned by HUF) are taxable for individuals at 20% rate."

HUF can pay salary to its members if they are contributing to its functioning and work of the joint Hindu family business. This salary expense can be deducted from the income of HUF. It can collect rent from members as well.



#### Attachments
**MC article** (0.00 kb) [download](http://www.moneycontrol.com/news/business/personal-finance-business/how-can-huf-help-individual-to-save-income-tax-1264531.html)

**http://mukeshraj.com/faq/** (0.00 kb) [download](http://Legal)

**http://mukeshraj.com/faq/** (0.00 kb) [download](http://FAQ)

### [132] IRA withdrawal plan

**Created:** 11/20/2017 2:51:47 PM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



#### Comments
**11/20/2017 2:59:20 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

[ET article](https://economictimes.indiatimes.com/nri/returning-to-india/nri-back-in-india-heres-what-to-do-with-your-401k-plans/articleshow/11631199.cms?intenttarget=no) :

- File return in both countries (US + India).
- Regular IRA and 401k
  - lumpsum withdrawal at senior age - 30% for non resident aliens of the US + India tax - US tax.
  - monthly pension: Article 20 of the DTAA provides that any private pensions and annuities (does not include social security benefits or public pensions) received will be taxed only in the country in which the taxpayer is a resident.

- Roth IRA - no US tax, only India tax.

- General non retirement funds: income earned abroad can be brought to India tax free within 7 years


#### Attachments
**ET article** (0.00 kb) [download](https://economictimes.indiatimes.com/nri/returning-to-india/nri-back-in-india-heres-what-to-do-with-your-401k-plans/articleshow/11631199.cms?intenttarget=no)

### [106] supratyaya: Freeze credit-checks

**Created:** 10/16/2017 4:00:04 PM

**Created by:** 

**Due:** 11/30/2018 12:00:00 PM

**Description:**

Context: Equifax leak

According to [this site](https://krebsonsecurity.com/2016/01/the-lowdown-on-freezing-your-kids-credit/), credit agencies aren't obliged to accept freeze-instructions of CA parents. But, according to [this page](http://clark.com/personal-finance-credit/credit-freeze-for-child/),  Experian and Equifax allow credit freezes for children in all 50 states.

according to [this page](http://clark.com/personal-finance-credit/credit-freeze-for-child/): "According to the Identity Theft Resource Center, kids are 51 times more likely to be the subject of identity theft than adults! Another study found that one in 10 kids has his or her identity stolen by the age of 18."

#### Checklist

[ ] Equifax: Check, enroll and freeze at https://trustedidpremier.com/eligibility/eligibility.html

[ ] Transunion freeze: https://www.transunion.com/credit-freeze/place-credit-freeze

[ ] Create initial fraud alert (across all 3 credit agencies), renew periodically: https://fraud.transunion.com 

[ ] Innovis

[ ] PRBC

#### Comments
**10/27/2017 5:24:59 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Equifax [says](https://www.freeze.equifax.com/Freeze/jsp/SFF_FrzMinorChild.jsp): "Generally an individual under the age of 18 does not have a credit file. If you believe your child's information has been used to obtain credit, please mail a letter of explanation with a copy of the following to the address shown below"

**10/16/2017 1:35:50 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Experian freeze - 10$.

**9/3/2018 3:49:49 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

https://www.quora.com/Visas-entry-exit-permits-After-how-many-days-can-a-person-re-enter-the-US-on-a-B2-visitor-visa-after-staying-there-for-5-months
Incident: one my friend mother used to travel like this 6 months in usa and 2/3 months in India & back to usa ( her daughter was studying in usa plus working legally, so once after couple of travels they stopped her and asked what is the reason of your frequent visits and long stays. She honestly told the truth. They made her sit there for 2/3 hours for reprocessing of her visa , thy cancelled her B1B2 visa, and reissued a single entry visa and told her that reapply for proper applicable category.

**9/3/2018 3:48:44 PM Shruthi Viswanath**

https://www.quora.com/How-long-do-I-have-to-wait-before-I-can-come-back-to-the-US-after-a-6-month-stay-using-a-tourist-visa

Technically no minimum wait period, but every time you make entry you have to convince the immigration officer that your purpose for entry is legitimate tourism, rather than an attempt to illegally reside in the United States. If you fail to convince the immigration officer this (and the burden of proof is always on you), your entry will be denied.Obviously, the shorter that time, the more likely the immigration officer will be suspicious. This is especially true if you have a pattern of long visits broken only by short trips home.

Passport validity paryAptam asti iti jJNAtam.

US Visa interview waiver program - http://www.ustraveldocs.com/in/in-niv-visarenew.asp#qualifications - "If I am applying for any other class of visa, my prior visa in the same class is still valid or expired within the last 12 months." इति वर्तते। 

अतः पश्चाद् एव नवीकृते चिन्ता नास्ति।

**9/10/2018 1:49:12 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Six Months Passport Validity Rule forentering the U.S. on non-immigrant visa. Visitors traveling to the United States are required to be in possession of passportsthat are valid for six months beyond the period of their intended stay in the United States.

**9/10/2018 11:33:34 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

@vasukikadabarajan - तव पारपत्रस्यापि (passport-अस्य) चित्रं प्रेषय।

**9/10/2018 11:23:57 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

https://www.quora.com/How-many-months-before-my-visa-expires-can-I-travel-to-the-US - न नवीकृतं चेदपि प्रयातुं शक्नोतीति।

### [189] प्राध्यापकेभ्यः भाषणम्

**Created:** 3/2/2018 5:08:29 PM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



**Description:**

```
Vishvas Vasuki has been developing the Vedavaapi software platform and its APIs for various sanskrit language services over the past year. He'll give an overview of the goals of the vedavaapi project, design rationale and architecture. He will introduce various services that Vedavaapi API currently provides including those of external collaborators working on 

He will give us a tour the GitHub repository of vedavaapi, the various modules over there and how to use them.

    Vedavaapi ullekhanam platform: Goals, architecture, usage
    Vedavaapi REST API sets created so far, example usage, demo
    Create awareness of various projects by sanskrit-programmers that are relevant to us: Dhaval, Kartikeyan, DCS etc.
    The external developers & their projects we are working with, and whose tools we can invoke via our APIs.
    Overview of the functionality of various github sub-projects under Vedavaapi: sanskrit-lttoolbox, sanskrit_data, scala-akka-http-server, scala-play-server, vedavaapi-chef.
```

  RewriteCond %{SERVER_NAME} =api.vedavaapi.org
  RewriteRule ^ https://%{SERVER_NAME}%{REQUEST_URI} [END,NE,R=permanent]

<VirtualHost *:80>

  CustomLog ${APACHE_LOG_DIR}/access.log combined

```

### [63] [archived] Fuller, combined API docs

**Created:** 7/24/2017 8:52:34 PM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः

**Due:** 9/22/2017 12:00:00 PM

#### Comments
**7/24/2017 8:57:29 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Currently, only some endpoints are documented using flask restplus, and that too is fragmented (ullekhanam is separate from textract etc..). Plain flask API (eg: oauth login) should be documented.

One needs to set up swagger UI which combines [api.__schema__](http://flask-restplus.readthedocs.io/en/stable/swagger.html) with other docs from https://github.com/gangverk/flask-swagger and then use https://github.com/swagger-api/swagger-ui to show the docs.

### [156] Upgrade server ubuntu

**Created:** 12/11/2017 11:16:49 AM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



**Description:**

Motivation - running sanskrit_parser on wsgi requires python 3.6, which is default on newer ubuntu version.

#### Comments
**12/11/2017 11:16:54 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**


If you continue, an additional ssh daemon will be started at port 
'1022'. 
Do you want to continue? 

Continue [yN] y

Starting additional sshd 

To make recovery in case of failure easier, an additional sshd will 
be started on port '1022'. If anything goes wrong with the running 
ssh you can still connect to the additional one. 
If you run a firewall, you may need to temporarily open this port. As 
this is potentially dangerous it's not done automatically. You can 
open the port with e.g.: 
'iptables -I INPUT -p tcp --dport 1022 -j ACCEPT' 

To continue please press [ENTER]

### [98] Separate Ullekhanam files repository

**Created:** 9/12/2017 12:18:05 PM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः

**Due:** 11/17/2017 12:00:00 PM

**Description:**

ullekhanam reads from and uploads books to a certain directory (currently /opt/scan2text/data/books ), often initialized with the sample-repository that comes with textract. This should not be the case for deployment on vedavaapi.

we should separate out a test/ development datastore from the production datastore - this already happens in the backend (although I should move the two example books to the test datastore )

### [128] त्वा-तुमुन्-प्रत्ययान्त-कोश-प्राप्तिः

**Created:** 11/10/2017 11:32:14 AM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः

**Due:** 11/16/2017 12:00:00 PM

#### Comments
**12/1/2017 10:58:15 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/14UEZmuSvbbdxAnqpZdSvSH8hrp3flPhPoo01aSXhbDY/edit#gid=1652568209  इत्यत्र पुष्पामातुः कृदन्तकोशो विद्यते सुष्ठूट्टङ्कितः। वाक्यनिर्माणयन्त्रादाव् उपयोगाय स्यात्।
 

**11/15/2017 3:40:33 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

यथासम्भवम् [पत्रेऽस्मिन्](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1Vbyf11ZI2BvPpr-QJt2g3fssjS99Z1ME3jJvUjRYzuM/edit#gid=1341588380)  विशिष्टरूपाण्य् उद्धृतानि त्वान्तानाम् नुमुनन्तानाञ्च कृदन्तरूपमालायाः। शिष्टानि स्रोतोऽन्तराद् वा, "धातुसादृश्य"-स्तम्भस्याधारेण पूर्याणि (येन्त्रेण मनुष्यैर् वा)।

**11/14/2017 4:43:59 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

परिष्कृतरूपसङ्ग्रहणे जनार्दनहेग्गडॆमहोदयः‌ पृष्टः - न तत्र फलम्  उत्पश्यामि।

**11/14/2017 4:32:24 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

कृदन्तरूपमालायाः‌ परिष्कृतरूपाणि लभ्यानि। 

- यान्त्रिकरीत्या कानिचन पदानि स्वीकर्तुं शक्यानि ([यथात्र](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1Vbyf11ZI2BvPpr-QJt2g3fssjS99Z1ME3jJvUjRYzuM/edit#gid=0) प्रायते), शिष्टानि तु कैश्चित् संस्कृतज्ञैः पूरणीयानि।

- गॆरार्डक्षेत्रे च लभ्यन्ते ऽपरिष्कृतानि कानिचन रूपाणि। ततोऽपि गृहीतुं शक्यम्, किन्तु सन्दिग्धानि। 

मह्यं‌ त्वादिममार्ग एव रोचते।

**11/10/2017 2:05:43 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

@saisusarla  तुमुनन्तानि लभ्यन्ते [ऽत्र](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/kmadathil/inriaxmlwrapper/master/SL_final.xml)।  "gantum" इत्यन्वेषताम्।

### [149] सामवेद-ग्रन्थ-प्रकाशनम्

#### Checklist

#### Comments
**11/8/2018 2:05:26 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

मुरलीकृष्णस्त्व् अनासक्तो भाति।

**11/8/2018 2:05:14 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

विद्युत्पुस्तकोत्पादनविधिर् दर्शितः। अग्रे स्वयम् प्रचिकाशयिषति माम् अनवलम्ब्य॥


**6/4/2018 8:35:35 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

गिरिजाप्रसाद-षडङ्गिनः सम्पर्कः साधितः। स बोधनीयः‌ कथं प्रकाशनीयानि पुस्तकानीति।

**4/1/2018 3:59:30 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

इत्थम् प्रार्थितम् -

https://youtu.be/frKzvspAv2M?list=PLhPjckGlZ7rRn7K_TC3oeRU6BHto8grV1&t=387 - अत्र दृश्यमानस्य मुरलीकृष्णश्रौतिनस् सम्पर्कं साधयितुम् इच्छामि। सामग्रन्थप्रकाशनप्रचारेषु सहकर्तुम् ईहे स्वतान्त्रिककौशलम् उपयुज्य।  तत्रभवान् Venugopalan @Sidd68 Harish हरीशः स्वामिनाथसुतः वा सहकरोत्व् इति याचे।

### [121] श्रौतसूत्रव्याख्या-प्रसारनम् अन्तर्जाले

**Created:** 1/26/2018 7:48:31 AM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



#### Checklist

[ ] मत्तूरुग्रामस्य श्रौतकर्मविवरणानाम् ३ ग्रन्थाः

[ ] मत्तूरुग्रामस्य श्रौतसूत्रव्याख्यायाः १ प्रतिः

[ ] http://vajpay.com/ ग्रन्थाः

#### Comments
**1/30/2018 10:50:07 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

नारायणवाजपेयी स्मारितो वाट्साप्-माध्यमेन।
मत्तूरु-रामनाथावधानिना श्यामार्यानुमतिर् लब्धा तद्रामस्थ-कृति-प्रकाशने।
तेषु श्रौतकर्मविवरणानाम् ३ ग्रन्थाः, श्रौतसूत्रव्याख्यायाः १ प्रतिः।


**1/26/2018 5:13:46 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

 http://vajpay.com/ इति भावत्कं जालक्षेत्रम् दृष्टम्। तत्र ननु सहर्षं ज्ञातो भवतोर् आपस्तम्बश्रौतसूत्रभाष्यप्रकाशने यत्नः। वर्धताम् अभिवर्धताम्! लोकोऽयम् अनुगृह्यते भवता, भवान् ह्यन्वर्थको भाति ब्राह्मणो ऽस्मद्देशे।

अत्र कश्चन प्रस्तावः। युगेऽस्मिन्न् अन्तर्जाले पुस्तकानां वितरणं सरलम्। जङ्गमयन्त्रैश्च तेषाम् अवलोकनम् अपि। क्वचिद् अग्न्याधाने साक्षात् तन्मया दृष्टमपि - यद् विवादपरिहारार्थं जङ्गमयन्त्रेण किमप्य् अन्तर्जालपुस्तकम् अवलोकितम् ऋत्विग्भ्याम्। तथा जिज्ञासवः शब्दशो ऽन्वेष्टुम् अपि ननु शक्नुवन्तीति विशेषः (-यथा "सोमक्रये" ऽखिलेऽपि श्रौतवाङ्मये क्व किमुक्तम् इति)। उदाहरणम् ईक्षताम् - गृह्यसूत्राणि टीकान्वितानि लभ्यन्ते (आर्कैवि अत्र। गूगल-प्ले-क्षेत्रे अत्र। Wiki.) । पाञ्चरात्रागमेषु http://www.kriyasagaram.in/ इत्यपरमुदाहरणम्। एवं मुक्तरीत्या भवद्भ्यां सृज्यमान्य् अपि पुस्तकानि लभ्येरन्न् इति काङ्क्षा मे।

भवद्भिरेवोक्तम् " There is also no real monetary profit to be made from the publication of such books. As such, it should not need to be said that in this noble effort to bring out rare texts, the support of the astika public is very much necessary.... For traditional pathashalas functioning under individual public contributions, we can provide the books at a lesser rate. Kindly note however that in any case profit is not being made from this and any funds obtained are going to help future publications."। युक्तमेतत्! विद्याविक्रयो मा भूत्। अन्तर्जाले मुक्तप्रकाशनेन भवतो बाधा स्यादिति नैव स्याच् छङ्का काचित्। धनाभावान्न कदाचिदपि भविष्यत्प्रकाशनोद्यमास् स्युः स्तम्भिताः वाम्। तदर्थं सिद्धाः स्यामैव वयमास्तिकाः। न च कागदपुस्तकान्यनेन भवेयुर् दुर्लभानि। किञ्च पुस्तकान्यन्तर्जाले सुलभानि स्युर् इत्यधिको लाभ आस्तिकजगत एव। अत्र चिन्तयित्वा स्वाभिप्रायं प्रकटयतु धीमन्। कथम् प्रकाशनीयम्, क्व प्रकाशनीयम् इत्यादौ मा भूच्चिन्ता - सर्वं तत् सुलभम् - निश्चिते पश्चात् परिहर्तुम् उचितम्।

इति प्रस्तावः प्रेषितः। मत्तूरुरामनाथो ऽपि ज्ञापितः।

### [178] मत्तूरु-योजना-प्रचारः

**Created:** 7/29/2018 7:38:01 AM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



#### Checklist

[x] जालक्षेत्र-सृष्टिः 8/6/2018 2:37:24 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः

[x] Indiafacts-क्षेत्रे प्रकाशनम् 11/8/2018 1:52:38 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः

[ ] Indic activists साहाय्यम्

[x] मोहित-प्रश्नः 11/8/2018 1:52:43 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः

#### Comments
**11/8/2018 1:53:25 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

न किञ्चिद् अस्माज् जातम्। किञ्च दत्तराजदेशपाण्डेय-सूचनानुसारं धनं गुरुकुलान्दोलनाल् लभ्यम् इति प्रयासस् त्यक्तः।

**8/8/2018 1:17:09 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

india-facts-नीतिनः सूचितः। सो ऽङ्ग्यकरोत्।

**8/6/2018 2:47:03 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

व्योम-सुहृद-वृन्द इत्थं सूचितम् -

सज्जनेभ्यो नमस्काराः। व्योमसंस्थया न सम्बद्धोऽयं सन्देशः, किञ्च तत्रत्यैः कैश्चित् सम्बद्धैः कार्यान्तरैस् स्यात् सम्बद्ध इति प्रश्नः। (विशिष्य @Venkata subramanian P वेङ्कट-सुब्रह्मण्यः व्योम-संस्थपकः  @vishvanAthaH विश्वनाथः व्योम-नेता @raghunandanaH padyapriyaH  इत्येतेषाम् अवधानाय।) https://sanskrit.github.io/matturu/contribute/veda-shaalaa.html इति किमपि सृष्टम् मया तत्रत्यैर् मन्त्रयित्वा। परिशील्य कथमेतेषां साहाय्यं कुर्यामेति चिन्तयन्तु।

**8/6/2018 2:38:31 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

इत्थं सन्देशः प्रेषितः केभ्यश्चिद् दिनेभ्यः प्राक् -

समवेतेभ्यस् सज्जनेभ्यो विनम्रा नमस्काराः।

श्यामार्येण सह यथा चर्चितं, तथा किञ्चिज् जालक्षेत्रम् असृजम् ( https://sanskrit.github.io/matturu/index.html#intro ) । उद्देशः - श्रीमता मोहितमहाशयेन ( http://indiafacts.org/after-millenia-tradition-reborn-vaidika-bharata/ ) + अन्यैश्च  यथा सत्कार्याणाङ्कृते धनं सङ्गृहीतम्, तथैव मत्तूरु-संशोधन-केन्द्रम् अपि कुर्याद् इति।

- मोहित @मोहितो भारद्वाजः माध्यन्दिनशाखाध्यायी mohito bhaaradvaajaH noiDa-vaasii veda-samarthakaH - तव विजयनगरयात्रायाः परम् लब्धे ऽवकाशे https://sanskrit.github.io/matturu/contribute/veda-shaalaa.html इति परिशील्य स्वाभिप्रायम् ब्रूहि। Indic activist जानानाञ्च सम्पर्कङ्कारय।

- @Rajaram Murthy mattur - ग्रामे कश्चन सामाजिकान्तर्जालेषु संलग्नः, सङ्गणकादौ निपुणो वैदिक एतादृशाय प्रचार-धनसङ्ग्रहणादि-कार्याय सिद्धस् स्यादिति मया सूचितम्, श्यामार्येण चोररीकृतम्। भवान् वा भवतः पुत्रो वा पात्रम् इदं निर्वहेत्? एवञ्च, सम्प्रति श्यामार्याय जालक्षेत्रम् इदं निवेद्य सानुवादं किं लिखितम् इति कथयित्वा तदीयाभिप्रायं whatsapp voice message द्वारा गृहीत्वा प्रेषणीयम्। तत्रापि भवत्परिवारं शरणं यामि। स्वानुकूल्यं सूचयतु 🙏

========

उत्तरं नैतावल्लब्धम्।

**Description:**

[mahAbhArata-mUla-paThanam.json](http://api.vedavaapi.org/scala/podcasts/v1/archiveRequests?archiveRequestUri=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fsanskrit-coders%2Frss-feeds%2Fraw%2Fmaster%2Ffeeds%2Fsa%2FrequestJsons%2FmahAbhArata-mUla-paThanam.json) feed fails.

```

### [197] anki- import from arbitrary url-s

**Created:** 9/19/2018 6:18:20 PM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



#### Comments
**9/19/2018 6:18:58 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Created a [discussion](https://anki.tenderapp.com/discussions/ankidesktop/29834-feature-request-import-from-arbitrary-url-s) in the support site.

"Hi!

Besides "Get Shared", there ought to be another button - Import from URL - which might point to some csv or even files like those hosted on ankiweb .

A use-case: Many of my decks were deleted from the ankiweb.net for lack of downloads and inactivity. If such users could conveniently store such niche creations elsewhere (eg github) which they could easily access directly by pasting the url in Anki desktop, they'd be better served.
"

## दीर्घ-कालीनम्

### [148] Investigate anonymous hard-to-censor social networks

**Created:** 3/27/2018 5:05:35 PM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



**Description:**

Data portability a plus.

#### Comments
**3/28/2018 11:24:34 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Precautions while using Tor: https://www.torproject.org/download/download.html#warning

You need to change some of your habits, as some things won't work exactly as you are used to.

Use Tor Browser
Tor does not protect all of your computer's Internet traffic when you run it. Tor only protects your applications that are properly configured to send their Internet traffic through Tor. To avoid problems with Tor configuration, we strongly recommend you use the Tor Browser. It is pre-configured to protect your privacy and anonymity on the web as long as you're browsing with Tor Browser itself. Almost any other web browser configuration is likely to be unsafe to use with Tor.

Don't torrent over Tor
Torrent file-sharing applications have been observed to ignore proxy settings and make direct connections even when they are told to use Tor. Even if your torrent application connects only through Tor, you will often send out your real IP address in the tracker GET request, because that's how torrents work. Not only do you deanonymize your torrent traffic and your other simultaneous Tor web traffic this way, you also slow down the entire Tor network for everyone else.

Don't enable or install browser plugins
Tor Browser will block browser plugins such as Flash, RealPlayer, Quicktime, and others: they can be manipulated into revealing your IP address. Similarly, we do not recommend installing additional addons or plugins into Tor Browser, as these may bypass Tor or otherwise harm your anonymity and privacy.

Use HTTPS versions of websites
Tor will encrypt your traffic to and within the Tor network, but the encryption of your traffic to the final destination website depends upon on that website. To help ensure private encryption to websites, Tor Browser includes HTTPS Everywhere to force the use of HTTPS encryption with major websites that support it. However, you should still watch the browser URL bar to ensure that websites you provide sensitive information to display a blue or green URL bar button, include https:// in the URL, and display the proper expected name for the website. Also see EFF's interactive page explaining how Tor and HTTPS relate.

Don't open documents downloaded through Tor while online
Tor Browser will warn you before automatically opening documents that are handled by external applications. DO NOT IGNORE THIS WARNING. You should be very careful when downloading documents via Tor (especially DOC and PDF files, unless you use the PDF viewer that's built into Tor Browser) as these documents can contain Internet resources that will be downloaded outside of Tor by the application that opens them. This will reveal your non-Tor IP address. If you must work with DOC and/or PDF files, we strongly recommend either using a disconnected computer, downloading the free VirtualBox and using it with a virtual machine image with networking disabled, or using Tails. Under no circumstances is it safe to use BitTorrent and Tor together, however.

Use bridges and/or find company
Tor tries to prevent attackers from learning what destination websites you connect to. However, by default, it does not prevent somebody watching your Internet traffic from learning that you're using Tor. If this matters to you, you can reduce this risk by configuring Tor to use a Tor bridge relay rather than connecting directly to the public Tor network. Ultimately the best protection is a social approach: the more Tor users there are near you and the more diverse their interests, the less dangerous it will be that you are one of them. Convince other people to use Tor, too!


Be smart and learn more. Understand what Tor does and does not offer. This list of pitfalls isn't complete, and we need your help identifying and documenting all the issues.

**3/28/2018 11:00:17 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

IP address can be masked with Tor. On chrome, this is easy with 
Kronymous + SwitchyOmega extensions.

IP address logging being ubiquitous, this seems unavoidable.

From [this thread](https://twitter.com/agnimaan/status/979057357002027009)

**3/28/2018 10:50:10 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

- From grub console
- from boot disk.

Loss - roughly half a day.

When I try to import https://github.com/vvasuki/movie_db_py/blob/master/data/movie_data_rinema.csv at https://www.rinema.com/agnimaan/uploads , I get: ​https://i.imgur.com/jm1mqG0.png . Reported to rinema.


**3/12/2018 6:40:57 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

tmdb seems promising. doesn't have export feature yet.

API seems attractive though - https://www.themoviedb.org/documentation/api . Many wrappers too.

**3/12/2018 6:16:08 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Rinema allows csv import / export. Import requires release year.

#### Comments

कश्चित् भार्गवः:
आपस्तम्बगृह्यसूत्र-गृह्यतात्पर्यदर्शन-टीकायाम्  "स्वयं दृष्ट्वा तृतीयां जपेत् ॥ आपस्तम्बगृह्यसूत्र ४.३ ॥"  इत्यत्र- "जपश्च सर्वत्र चातुस्स्वर्येण न तु करणमन्त्रादिवदेकश्रुत्या । एकश्रुति दूरात्सम्बुद्धौ(पा.सू.१२३३)  यज्ञकर्मण्यजपन्यूखसामसुऽ(पा.सू.१२३४) इति वचनात् ।"

**7/27/2018 4:32:44 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

प्रयाण आचारः - श्रौतम् स्मार्तम्

**7/26/2018 7:19:50 AM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

सरलतमसोमानुष्ठाने प्रश्नः।

सद्यस्करयागः सरलतमः?
कियान् व्ययः?
स्वीया भूमिर् आवश्यकी?

**4/9/2018 7:16:27 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Taittiriya Aranyaka IV.38 -→ अस्य विनियोगे प्रश्नः।                        
"गत्वैनमभिव्याहरेत्" इत्यत्र - "स यथा श्रुणुयात् तथाभिव्याहरेद्" इति निर्देशो वा?                        
(मरून्मत्तशत्रून् एवम् अभिचरितुमिच्छामि काले)

**4/9/2018 7:15:39 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

गोसवे मातृगमनचोदनम्??

[10:12, 2/4/2017] +1 (512) 524-6901: 
अपरेयं प्रार्थना - श्यामण्णगुरोर् अत्रान्तिमे वाक्ये विचारं जिज्ञासे -  Ap. XXII.13.1-3 - tene.s.tvaa samvatsaram pashuvrato bhavati / upaavahaayodakam pibet t.r.naani caacchindyaat / upa maataram iyaad upa svasaaram upa sagotraam / इत्यनेन किं गम्यत इति तदभिप्रायः? अपि युवयोर् अन्यतरस् तस्माज् ज्ञात्वा ब्रूयात्?                        

==============

तथा च - "चतुर्दिनात्मकविवाहं विनाऽग्निं उपासितुं न भवत्य् अर्हता" इत्यत्र प्रमाणानि तर्कञ्च जिज्ञासे।

Search options - 

- https://github.com/christian-fei/Simple-Jekyll-Search does not look at contents
- google custom site search is not instant.
- lunar.js - instant but heavy(?) on client side - https://learn.cloudcannon.com/jekyll/jekyll-search-using-lunr-js/ ( plugin-  https://github.com/slashdotdash/jekyll-lunr-js-search )
- algolia community - https://github.com/algolia/jekyll-algolia


**5/18/2018 10:36:10 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Potential jekyll themes - 
https://idratherbewriting.com/documentation-theme-jekyll/mydoc_sidebar_navigation.html
https://github.com/daattali/beautiful-jekyll#showcased-users-success-stories
Editing links in layout from http://jekyllthemes.org/themes/git-wiki-for-documentation/
HTML5 mobile friendliness - https://github.com/chrisbobbe/jekyll-theme-prologue

### [119] goodreads for music: scrobbing

**Created:** 4/15/2018 9:40:47 PM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



#### Comments
**4/15/2018 9:53:47 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Installed web scrobbler extension - https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/web-scrobbler/hhinaapppaileiechjoiifaancjggfjm/related

based on tip from https://community.spotify.com/t5/forums/v3_1/forumtopicpage/board-id/spotifyaccountrelated/thread-id/267974/page/3 . working now.

**4/15/2018 9:52:13 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Another alternative is libre.fm

**4/15/2018 9:46:54 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

With spotify apps (but not web client), can set up scrobbling to last.fm.
https://support.spotify.com/us/using_spotify/app_integrations/scrobble-to-last-fm/

last.fm data can be exported to csv using their API.

### [111] whatsapp web - phone not connected samasyA

**Created:** 4/3/2018 1:54:48 PM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः



**Description:**

This is what I get most of the time on web.whatsapp.com these days, which prevents me from responding or proposing as much as I would like. Always half broken, slow.

#### Comments
**4/3/2018 2:04:37 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

"Another option (for those users with Android 6.0 or higher) is to go to Settings > Battery, but then press the option button and select "optimize battery usage". You can switch between "apps not optimized" and "all apps". Select the second one and turn on or off WhatsApp.
" इति दृष्टम् [इतः](https://webapps.stackexchange.com/questions/87858/whatsapp-web-phone-not-connected)। तदपि प्रयते।

**4/3/2018 1:56:44 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Project Fi has long been disabled. Still, it seems that phone was trying to connect via LTE. 
Disabling phone data made things better (refreshing whatsapp on phone synced whatsapp web).

### [96] उत्तरा कथा-रक्षण-व्यवस्था

**Created:** 3/1/2018 4:46:40 PM

**Created by:** Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः

**Due:** 3/4/2018 12:00:00 PM

**Description:**

Problem with google spreadsheet:
- Clumsy editing of big text.

Desiderata:
Easy editing - online, not just on linux computer.
Good querying and filtering.
Version control. 
Backed up data.


#### Comments
**3/3/2018 9:26:38 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

antato gatvA airtable iti chitam.

**3/3/2018 8:35:03 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

[image.png](https://trello-attachments.s3.amazonaws.com/596e1eb8651766e7206282de/5a989ef06defb8f1a263e9d2/8f521662620e9116acd306ee6d9b399f/image.png) 

Idea: Use hosted Mongodb .
Disadvantage: 512 MB data limit. No backup.

**3/3/2018 8:31:07 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

[image.png](https://trello-attachments.s3.amazonaws.com/596e1eb8651766e7206282de/5a989ef06defb8f1a263e9d2/3ab8e3c5b0a2eb235503ab768e8b9a72/image.png) 
Idea: Google datastore free quota
Disadvantage: Pricing (consider backup and restore) is a bit icky.

**3/3/2018 8:06:16 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Idea: Airtable (evernote does not allow custom fields as of 2017)
Advantage: good 2 week revision history
Disadvantage: 1200 records in the free plan only. 

**3/3/2018 7:22:15 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Idea: Private wikidata instance.
Disadvantage: Too heavy, need a server. Importing can be a chore.
Advantage: Version control. Easy editing. Good querying.

**3/2/2018 5:06:02 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Idea: Private wiki with yaml content.

https://confluence.atlassian.com/bitbucket/wikis-221449748.html

**3/1/2018 5:40:20 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Idea: yaml based page at vvasuki.bitbucket.io

Rest same as "Idea: use rahaShTippaNyaH private repo on bitbucket."


**3/1/2018 5:26:24 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Idea: Simply use FastoNoSQL with unqlite.
Disadvantage: Stuck to laptop. No good.

**3/1/2018 5:24:48 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Idea: Simply use the yaml file, with a good GUI (eg: atom with plugin).

**3/1/2018 5:16:24 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Idea: Keep in google spreadhsheet
Add a UI (using some JS lib)
Test entry is still not ideal.

Option: use https://www.prolificoaktree.com/cloud-software/20-text-boxes-in-sheets or notes or comments - but that results in export problems.

**3/1/2018 4:50:40 PM Vishvas V विश्वासो वासुकिजः**

Idea: use rahaShTippaNyaH private repo on bitbucket.
Store data in yaml file.
Write a html+js viewer.

Advantage: can edit yaml anywhere.
Disadvantage: can only get the html view on local machine.

UI ideas:
https://www.webcomponents.org/element/LostInBrittany/granite-yaml
https://github.com/nodeca/js-yaml

Or use https://jekyllrb.com/docs/quickstart/ with _data folder.
